currency notional, underlying payment date, and payment date adjustment.\n122:    *\n123:    * @param longShort the long/short flag of the option\n124:    * @param expiry the option expiry\n125:    * @param currencyPair the FX currency pair\n126:    * @param putCall the put/call flag of the option\n127:    * @param strike the FX strike\n128:    * @param baseNotional the base currency notional amount: should always be positive\n129:    * @param paymentDate the payment date of the underlying FX cash flows\n130:    * @param paymentDateAdjustment the adjustment to apply to the payment date\n131:    * @return an equivalent fx vanilla option\n132:    */\n133:   public static FxVanillaOption of(\n134:       LongShort longShort,\n135:       ZonedDateTime expiry,\n136:       CurrencyPair currencyPair,\n137:       PutCall putCall,\n138:       double strike,\n139:       double baseNotional,\n140:       LocalDate paymentDate,\n141:       BusinessDayAdjustment paymentDateAdjustment) {\n142: \n143:     ArgChecker.isTrue(baseNotional > 0, \"Base notional must be positive\");\n144:     ArgChecker.isTrue(strike > 0, \"FX strike must be positive\");\n145: \n146:     // for a vanilla call, will be long the base currency and short the counter currency\n147:     // for a vanilla put, will be short the base currency and long the counter currency\n148:     double baseAmount = putCall.isCall() ? baseNotional : -baseNotional;\n149:     double counterNotional = strike * baseNotional;\n150:     double counterAmount = putCall.isCall() ? -counterNotional : counterNotional;\n151:     CurrencyAmount baseCurrencyAmount = CurrencyAmount.of(currencyPair.getBase(), baseAmount);\n152:     CurrencyAmount counterCurrencyAmount = CurrencyAmount.of(currencyPair.getCounter(), counterAmount);\n153:     FxSingle equivalentUnderlying = paymentDateAdjustment == null ?\n154:         FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate) :\n155:         FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate, paymentDateAdjustment);\n156: \n157:     return FxVanillaOption.builder()\n158:   * the long party, potentially enter into the inverse transaction.\n   */\n  @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\")\n  private final LongShort longShort;\n  /**\n   * The expiry date of the option\n   * @param expiry the option expiry\n   * @param currencyPair the FX currency pair\n   * @param putCall the put/call flag of the option\n   * @param strike the FX strike\n   * @param baseNotional the base currency notional amount: should always be positive\n   * @param paymentDate the payment date of the underlying FX cash flows\n   * @param paymentDateAdjustment the adjustment to apply to the payment date\n   * @return an equivalent fx european option\n   */\n  public static FxEuropeanOption of(\n      LongShort longShort,\n      ZonedDateTime expiry,\n      CurrencyPair currencyPair,\n      PutCall putCall,\n      double strike,\n      double baseNotional,\n      LocalDate paymentDate,\n      BusinessDayAdjustment paymentDateAdjustment) {\n\n    ArgChecker.isTrue(baseNotional > 0, \"Base notional must be positive\");\n    ArgChecker.isTrue(strike > 0, \"FX strike must be positive\");\n\n    // for a vanilla call, will be long the base currency and short the counter currency\n    // for a vanilla put, will be short the base currency and long the counter currency\n    double baseAmount = putCall.isCall() ? baseNotional : -baseNotional;\n    double counterNotional = strike * baseNotional;\n    double counterAmount = putCall.isCall() ? -counterNotional : counterNotional;\n    CurrencyAmount baseCurrencyAmount = paymentDateAdjustment == null ?\n        FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate) :\n        FxSingle.of(baseCurrencyAmount, counterCurrencyAmount, paymentDate, paymentDateAdjustment);\n\n    return FxEuropeanOption.builder()\n        .longShort(longShort)\n        .expiryDate(expiry.toLocalDate())\n        .expiryTime(expiry.toLocalTime())\n        .expiryZone(expiry.getZone())\n        .underlying(equivalentUnderlying)\n        .build();\n  }\n\n  //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n
